/home/eirikr/Github/tilix/term_analysis/wezterm/docs/scrollback.md:57:### Searching the scrollback
/home/eirikr/Github/tilix/term_analysis/wezterm/docs/scrollback.md:60:search overlay in the current tab.
/home/eirikr/Github/tilix/term_analysis/wezterm/docs/scrollback.md:62:When the search overlay is active the behavior of wezterm changes:
/home/eirikr/Github/tilix/term_analysis/wezterm/docs/scrollback.md:64:* Typing (or pasting) text will populate the *search pattern* in the bar at the bottom of the screen.
/home/eirikr/Github/tilix/term_analysis/wezterm/docs/scrollback.md:65:* Text from the scrollback that matches the *search pattern* will be highlighted and
/home/eirikr/Github/tilix/term_analysis/wezterm/docs/scrollback.md:66:  the number of matches shown in the search bar.
/home/eirikr/Github/tilix/term_analysis/wezterm/docs/scrollback.md:76:  The matching mode is indicated in the search bar.
/home/eirikr/Github/tilix/term_analysis/wezterm/docs/scrollback.md:77:* `CTRL-U` will clear the *search pattern* so you can start over.
/home/eirikr/Github/tilix/term_analysis/wezterm/docs/scrollback.md:79:* `Escape` will cancel the search overlay, leaving the currently selected text selected

/home/eirikr/Github/tilix/term_analysis/wezterm/docs/config/lua/keyassignment/ActivateKeyTable.md:14:    * {{since('20220807-113146-c2fee766', inline=True)}}: the timer is reset each time you press a key that matches this key table activation, allowing for repeated key presses
/home/eirikr/Github/tilix/term_analysis/wezterm/docs/config/lua/keyassignment/ActivateKeyTable.md:16:* `one_shot` - an optional boolean that controls whether the activation will pop itself after a single additional key press.  The default if left unspecified is `one_shot=true`. When set to `false`, pressing a key will not automatically pop the activation and you will need to use either a timeout or an explicit key assignment that triggers [PopKeyTable](PopKeyTable.md) to cancel the activation.
/home/eirikr/Github/tilix/term_analysis/wezterm/docs/config/lua/keyassignment/ActivateKeyTable.md:17:* `replace_current` - an optional boolean. Defaults to `false` if unspecified. If set to `true` then behave as though [PopKeyTable](PopKeyTable.md) was triggered before pushing this new activation on the stack.  This is most useful for key assignments in a table that was activated using `one_shot=false`.
